sbit	RDB	=	P3^6;

sbit	KEY =	P2^7;

//sbit  T_BUSY    = P3^7;  //touch sreen busy   1.0
sbit  T_DCLK    = P3^2;  //SPI CLOCK   1.4
sbit  T_DIN     = P3^1;  //SPI DATA IN
sbit  T_DOUT    = P2^1;  //SPI DATA OUT   1.3
sbit  T_IRQ     = P2^0;  //IRQ

/*********************touch screen end**************/
 void serial_delay()
{
	int i;
	for (i = 0;i<general_delay; i++ ){};
}


void TOUCH_RESET(void)
{
 T_DCLK=0;
 T_CS=1;
 T_DIN=0;
 T_DCLK=0;
 T_DOUT=0;
 T_CS=0;
 }


void ADS7843_SPI_Start( void )
{
 TP_DCLK(0);
 TP_CS(1);
 TP_DIN(1);
 TP_DCLK(1);
 TP_CS(0);
}

void ADS7843_Write (unsigned char cmd )
{
    unsigned char buf, i, j ;
    TP_DCLK(0);
	for( i = 0; i < 8; i++ )
	{
		buf = (cmd >> (7-i)) & 0x1 ;
		TP_DIN(buf);

		for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );
		TP_DCLK(1);

		for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );
		TP_DCLK(0);
	}
}


unsigned int ADS7843_Read ( void )
{
	unsigned int buf = 0 ;
	unsigned char i, j ;

	for( i = 0; i < 12; i++ )
	{
		buf = buf << 1 ;
		TP_DCLK(1);
		for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );
		TP_DCLK(0);
		for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );
		if ( TP_DOUT )
                buf = buf + 1 ;
                //TP_DCLK(0);
		for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );
	//for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );
	}
	for( i = 0; i < 4; i++ )
	{
		TP_DCLK(1);
		for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );		//200ns
		TP_DCLK(0);
		for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );
	}
	return( buf ) ;
}

void touch_panel_tuning(U16 coord1, U16 adc1,
                        U16 coord2, U16 adc2,
                        float *slope,     float *offset)
{
   *slope=(float)((coord2-coord1)/(adc2-adc1));
   *offset=(float)coord1-(*slope)*(float)adc1;
}

void ADS7843_disp()// interrupt 0 using 0
{
	long x, y;
	char j ;
	unsigned int px_max=0,py_max=0,px_min=0,py_min=0;
	x_slope=0.066;//0.066
	y_slope=0.090;//0.090
	x_offset = -15.18;
	y_offset = -25.83;

	for( j = 0; j < general_delay; j++ );
if (TP_IRQ == 0)
	{
		ADS7843_SPI_Start() ;
		for( j = 0; j < 5; j++ );
		//while ( TP_BUSY ) ;

		ADS7843_Write( CHX ) ;
		x = ADS7843_Read();//dummy
		ADS7843_Write( CHX ) ;
		x = ADS7843_Read();//dummy
		ADS7843_Write( CHX ) ;
		x += ADS7843_Read();//dummy
		x = x/2;
		x= 0.066 * (ADC_X_END - x);
//		x= 0.066 * (x-230);

		ADS7843_Write( CHY ) ;
		y = ADS7843_Read() ;
		ADS7843_Write( CHY ) ;
		y = ADS7843_Read() ;
		ADS7843_Write( CHY ) ;
		y += ADS7843_Read();//dummy
		y = y/2;

//		y= 0.0896 * (y - 287);//0.896
	    y= 0.0896 * (ADC_Y_END - y);//0.896
		//if( (x != 4095)&&(y != 4095)&&(x != 0)&&(y != 0) )
		//	{
				//x=x/(4095/240);
				//y=y/(4095/320);
				if(x<SCREEN_X_START)
					x=SCREEN_X_START;
				else if (x>SCREEN_X_END)
					x=SCREEN_X_END;

				if(y<SCREEN_Y_START)
					y=SCREEN_Y_START;
				else if (y>SCREEN_Y_END)
					y=SCREEN_Y_END;
				LCD_Color_with_ADD(0x07,0xE0,240-x,240-x+1,320-y,320-y+1);
		//	}
		TP_CS(1);
	}
}





void LCD_Color_with_ADD(char data1,char data2,int x1,int x2,int y1,int y2){
     unsigned char i,j;
//     unsigned char hor,ver;
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x50);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(x1);        //hs
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x51);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(x2);        //he
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x52);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(y1);        //vs
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x53);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(y2);        //ve

     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0000);
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0000);
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0000);
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0000);

     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x20);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(x1);        //h
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x21);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(y1);        //v
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x22);
	for(i=0;i<y2-y1+1;i++)
            for (j=0;j<x2-x1+1;j++)
			{
                        LCD_WRITE_DATA(data1,data2);
			}
	}



void DrawDot(unsigned int x_orgi,unsigned int y_orgi)
{
//	int i,j;
	int Pox,Poy,Px_bak,Py_bak;
//        unsigned char colorH,colorL;
        px_max=x_orgi>px_max?x_orgi:px_max; //get x(max)
        py_max=y_orgi>py_max?y_orgi:py_max; //get y(max)
        px_min=x_orgi>px_min?px_min:x_orgi; //get x(min)
        py_min=y_orgi<py_min?y_orgi:py_min; //get y(min)
	Px_bak=x_orgi;
	Py_bak=y_orgi;
	Pox=Px_bak/21;
	Poy=Py_bak/16;
	LCD_Color_with_ADD(0x07,0xE0,Pox,Pox+3,Poy,Poy+3);

}

void HD_reset(){
	RESETB=0;
	delayms(50);
	RESETB=1;
	delayms(10);
	}


  void LCD_INIT_ILI9335(void)
	{
//*********************************************Start intial Sequence	  	
		send_host_reg_command(0x0001,0x0100);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0002,0x0200);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0003,0x1030);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0008,0x0202);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0009,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x000A,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x000C,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x000D,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0060,0x2700);	
		send_host_reg_command(0x0061,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x006A,0x0000);
		delayms(10);
//*********************************************Power On
		send_host_reg_command(0x0010,0x1490);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0011,0x0227);
		delayms(80);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0012,0x000c);
		delayms(10);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0013,0x1000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0029,0x000b);
		send_host_reg_command(0x002b,0x000b);
		delayms(10);

		send_host_reg_command(0x0020,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0021,0x0000);
//*********************************************Set gamma
		send_host_reg_command(0x0030,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0031,0x0406);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0032,0x0002);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0035,0x0402);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0036,0x0004);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0037,0x0507);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0038,0x0103);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0039,0x0707);
		send_host_reg_command(0x003c,0x0204);
		send_host_reg_command(0x003d,0x0004);
//**********************************************Set Gram aera
		send_host_reg_command(0x0050,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0051,0x00ef);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0052,0x0000);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0053,0x013f);

		delayms(10);
		send_host_reg_command(0x0007,0x0133);
	}


void LCD_WRITE_CMD(char cmd1,char cmd2){
      RS = 0;
      RDB = 1;
      CSB = 0;

//      WRB = 0;
      DataBusH = cmd1;
      WRB = 0;
      WRB = 1;

//      WRB = 0;
      DataBusH = cmd2;
      WRB = 0;
      WRB = 1;
      CSB = 1;
	}

void LCD_WRITE_DATA(char dataa,char datab){
      RS = 1;
      RDB = 1;
      CSB = 0;

//      WRB = 0;
      DataBusH = dataa;
      WRB = 0;
      WRB = 1;

//      WRB = 0;
      DataBusH = datab;
      WRB = 0;
      WRB = 1;
      CSB = 1;
	}


void LCD_READ_ID(void){

      unsigned char idH,idL;
      DataBusH = 0xff;
      RS = 0;
      _nop_();
      CSB = 0;

      WRB = 1;
      RDB = 0;
      delayus(10);
      idH= DataBusH;
       RDB = 1;
      delayus(10);

      id  = idH;

	  idL= DataBusH;
	  RDB = 1;
      delayus(10);
      id  = (id<<8)|idL;
	  CSB = 1;
      RS  = 0;
	}

void LLCD_WRITE_CMD(int cmd){
      RS = 0;
      RDB = 1;
      CSB = 0;

//      WRB = 0;
      DataBusH = cmd>>8;
      WRB = 0;
      WRB = 1;

//      WRB = 0;
      DataBusH = cmd;
      WRB = 0;
      WRB = 1;
      CSB = 1;
	}

void LLCD_WRITE_DATA(int dataa){
      RS = 1;
      RDB = 1;
      CSB = 0;

//      WRB = 0;
      DataBusH = dataa>>8;
      WRB = 0;
      WRB = 1;

//      WRB = 0;
      DataBusH = dataa;
      WRB = 0;
      WRB = 1;
      CSB = 1;
	}


      
void send_host_reg_command(int cmd,int dataa)
     {
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(cmd);
     LLCD_WRITE_DATA(dataa);
     }



void adderset(int xs,int xe,int ys,int ye){

     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0050);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(xs);        //hs
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0051);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(xe);        //he
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0052);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(ys);        //vs
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0053);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(ye);        //ve


     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0020);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(xs);        //h
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0021);        LLCD_WRITE_DATA(ys);        //v
     LLCD_WRITE_CMD(0x0022);
}


void LCD_TEST_id(unsigned char *id){
     unsigned	char i,j,pixH,pixL;
       	 for (i=0;i<25;i++){
			for (j=0;j<25;j++){
				pixH=*id++;
				pixL=*id++;
				LCD_WRITE_DATA(pixH,pixL);
                                //LCD_WRITE_DATA(0xf8,0x00);
				}
		}

	}


void LCD_id_SHOW(int a,int b,int c,int d){

     adderset(0,25,0,25);
     LCD_TEST_id(s[a]);
     adderset(25,50,0,25);
     LCD_TEST_id(s[b]);
     adderset(50,75,0,25);
     LCD_TEST_id(s[c]);
     adderset(75,100,0,25);
     LCD_TEST_id(s[d]);

}


void LCD_TEST_SingleColor(char colorH,char colorL){
     int i,j;
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x50);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //hs
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x51);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0xef);        //he
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x52);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //vs
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x53);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x01,0x3f);        //ve


     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x20);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //h
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x21);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //v
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x22);

	 for (i=0;i<240;i++){
		for (j=0;j<320;j++){
			LCD_WRITE_DATA(colorH,colorL);
			}
		}
	}



void LCD_TEST_Picture1(unsigned char *picture1){
     unsigned	char i,j,pixH,pixL;

     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x50);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //hs 95f
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x51);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0xef);        //he
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x52);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //vs
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x53);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x01,0x3f);        //ve 00-09


     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x20);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //h
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x21);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //v
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x22);


       	 for (i=0;i<80;i++){
			for (j=0;j<240;j++){
				pixH=*picture1++;
				pixL=*picture1++;
				LCD_WRITE_DATA(pixH,pixL);
                                //LCD_WRITE_DATA(0xf8,0x00);
				}
		}

	}

void LCD_show_window(void){
     int i,j;
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x50);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //hs
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x51);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0xef);        //he
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x52);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //vs
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x53);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x01,0x3f);        //ve


     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x20);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //h
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x21);        LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);        //v
     LCD_WRITE_CMD(0x00,0x22);

	 for (i=0;i<1;i++){
		for (j=0;j<240;j++){
			LCD_WRITE_DATA(0xff,0xff);
			}
		}

	 for (i=0;i<318;i++){
		for (j=0;j<240;j++){
                if((j==0)||(j==239)){LCD_WRITE_DATA(0xff,0xff);}
                else
			{LCD_WRITE_DATA(0x00,0x00);}
			}
		}

	 for (i=0;i<1;i++){
		for (j=0;j<240;j++){
			LCD_WRITE_DATA(0xff,0xff);
			}
		}
	}
/*********************显示图片（从外部存储器）*******************************/
 
void display_eprom(unsigned char p)
{
	int i,d1,d2,k;
	unsigned int addr;	

	for(k=0;k<10;k++)
	{
	if(k<9)
		{
		addr=0x0000;		
		for(i=0;i<8192;i++)
			{
			   	d1=XBYTE[addr++];
				d2=XBYTE[addr++];
				LCD_WRITE_DATA(d1,d2);
				pic_select=(10*(p-1)+k);
			}
		}
	else
		{
		addr=0x0000;		
		for(i=0;i<3072;i++)
			{
                d1=XBYTE[addr++];
				d2=XBYTE[addr++];
				LCD_WRITE_DATA(d1,d2);
				pic_select=(10*(p-1)+k);
			}
		}
	}
} 

void Keypress()
	{
	while(KEY)
	delayms(10);
	}

void delayms(int value)
	{
	while (value){
		delayus(99);
		value--;
		}
	}

void delayus(int value1)
	{
	while (value1)

	value1--;
	}
